country_event = { # The American Legion Appointment
	id = unionstate.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event unionstate.1"}
	title = unionstate.1.t
	desc = unionstate.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers_watching

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = TEX
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
	}

	immediate = {
	hidden_effect = {
			# AuthDem Events
			country_event = {
				id = unionstate.13
				days = 150
				random = 20
			}
			country_event = {
				id = unionstate.16
				days = 210
				random = 30
			}
			country_event = {
				id = unionstate.18
				days = 270
				random = 40
			}
			country_event = {
				id = unionstate.20
				days = 330
				random = 50
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Terry de la Mesa Allen Jr
		name = unionstate.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
	}
	option = { # Sid McMath
		name = unionstate.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = AFP_leftism
			value = -1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TEX_leftism_tooltip
	}
	option = { # Gerald L.K. Smith
		name = unionstate.1.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TEX_rightism_tooltip
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = AFP_leftism
			value = 1
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The Long Dynasty
	id = unionstate.12
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event unionstate.12"}
	title = unionstate.12.t
	desc = unionstate.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_TEX_long_family

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = TEX
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		has_government = authoritarian_democrat
		has_country_leader = {
			ruling_only = yes
			name = "Huey Long"
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = TEX_Earl_Kemp_Long_hog_ade
			}
			NOT = {
				has_idea = TEX_Russell_Billiu_Long_sec_ade
			}
		}
		date > 1941.01.01
	}

	option = { # That's going too far
		name = unionstate.12.a
		add_stability = 0.01
	}
	option = { # You can't go wrong with Long
		name = unionstate.12.b
		add_stability = -0.03
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = TEX_Earl_Kemp_Long_hog_ade
				}
			}
			add_ideas = TEX_Earl_Kemp_Long_hog_ade
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = TEX_Russell_Billiu_Long_sec_ade
				}
			}
			add_ideas = TEX_Russell_Billiu_Long_sec_ade
		}
	}
}

}

country_event = { #Minutemen Want to Cancel Speech
	id = unionstate.51
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event unionstate.51"}
	title = unionstate.51.t
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
	OR = {
		has_completed_focus = TEX_imperial_presidency
		has_completed_focus = TEX_perfect_democracy
	}
	has_country_leader = {
		ruling_only = yes
		name = "Huey Long"
	}
	has_completed_focus = TEX_employment_expansion
	date > 1939.8.5
	}
	
	desc = {
	text = unionstate.51.d.left
	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = TEX_reconcile_the_left
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
	text = unionstate.51.d.right
	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = TEX_reconcile_the_right
		}
	}

	desc = {
	text = unionstate.51.d.alone
	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = TEX_afp_alone
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_TEX_Huey_Guards

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Safety First
		name = unionstate.51.a
		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = 0.05
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
	}
	option = { #No, I shall give my tour
		name = unionstate.51.b
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_political_power = 15
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = unionstate.5100
			days = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Huey Long's Trial of Assassins
	id = unionstate.5108
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event unionstate.5108"}
	title = unionstate.5108.t
	
	desc = { ###Smith Coup in the Capitol###
	text = unionstate.5108.d.coupsmith
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
		has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Gerald L.K. Smith" }
		}
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = AFP_smith_power
			value > 4
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = { ###Coughlin Coup in the Capitol###
	text = unionstate.5108.d.coupcoughlin
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
		has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Charles Coughlin" }
		}
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = AFP_coughlin_power
			value > 4
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = { ###Long Coup in the Capitol###
	text = unionstate.5108.d.couplong
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
		has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Earl Long" }
		}
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = AFP_long_power
			value > 4
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = { ###Bingham Coup in the Capitol###
	text = unionstate.5108.d.coupbingham
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
		has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Alfred Mitchell Bingham" }
		}
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = AFP_bingham_power
			value > 4
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = { ###Trial Proceeds as Planned###
	text = unionstate.5108.d.generic
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = AFP_smith_power
				value < 5
				}
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = AFP_coughlin_power
				value < 5
				}
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = AFP_long_power
				value < 5
				}
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = AFP_bingham_power
				value < 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	picture = GFX_event_TEX_Silver_Legion_grows

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Coup
		name = unionstate.5108.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
					has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Gerald L.K. Smith" }
					}
					has_country_flag = {
					flag = AFP_smith_power
					value > 4
					}
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
					has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Charles Coughlin" }
					}
					has_country_flag = {
					flag = AFP_coughlin_power
					value > 4
					}
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
					has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Earl Long" }
					}
					has_country_flag = {
					flag = AFP_long_power
					value > 4
					}
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
					has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Alfred Mitchell Bingham" }
					}
					has_country_flag = {
					flag = AFP_bingham_power
					value > 4
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
				has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Gerald L.K. Smith" }
				}
				has_country_flag = {
				flag = AFP_smith_power
				value > 4
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Gerald L.K. Smith"
				desc = "POLITICS_GERALD_LK_SMITH_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/TEX/Portrait_TEX_Gerald_L_K_Smith.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = pataut_longism_subtype
				traits = { propaganda_expert }
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
				has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Charles Coughlin" }
				}
				has_country_flag = {
				flag = AFP_coughlin_power
				value > 4
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Charles Coughlin"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHARLES_COUGHLIN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/TEX/Portrait_TEX_Charles_Coughlin.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"

				traits = { radio_preist }
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {

				has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Earl Long" }
				}
				has_country_flag = {
				flag = AFP_long_power
				value > 4
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Earl Long"

			}
		}
		else_if = {

				}
				has_country_flag = {
				flag = AFP_bingham_power
				value > 4
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Alfred Mitchell Bingham"

			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Normal Trial

	is_triggered_only = yes

		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		add_political_power = 10
		add_stability = 0.03
		add_command_power = 5
	}
}

country_event = { # Socialist terrorism - factory sabotaged
	id = unionstate.200
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event unionstate.200"}
	title = unionstate.200.t
	desc = unionstate.200.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SRI_bombing

	trigger = {
		tag = TEX
		OR = {
			has_idea = ACW_socialist_resistance_1
			has_idea = ACW_socialist_resistance_2
			has_idea = ACW_socialist_resistance_3
			has_idea = ACW_socialist_resistance_4
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			OR = {
				is_core_of = USA
				is_core_of = CSA
				is_core_of = TEX
				is_core_of = CAL
			}
			industrial_complex > 0
			is_controlled_by = TEX
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 45
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			has_idea = ACW_socialist_resistance_2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_idea = ACW_socialist_resistance_3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_idea = ACW_socialist_resistance_4
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = USA
						is_core_of = CSA
						is_core_of = TEX
						is_core_of = CAL
					}
					industrial_complex > 0

country_event = { # Wedding
	id = cathdeath.105
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event cathdeath.102" }
	title = cathdeath.105.t
	desc = cathdeath.105.d
	picture = GFX_event_TEX_princess_wedding

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #soccon
		name = cathdeath.105.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TEX_germ_prince
				GER = {
					exists = yes
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				TEX = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = TEX
					NOT = {
						is_subject_of = TEX
					}
				}
				GER = {
				add_to_faction = PREV
				}
			}
			GER = {
				add_to_faction = TEX
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TEX_germ_prince
				GER = {
					exists = yes
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				TEX = {
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
			}
			GER = {
				add_to_faction = TEX
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TEX_germ_prince
				GER = {
					exists = yes
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
				TEX = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			TEX = {
				add_to_faction = GER
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TEX_austrian_prince
				AUS = {
					exists = yes
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				TEX = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = TEX
					NOT = {
						is_subject_of = TEX
					}
				}
				AUS = {
				add_to_faction = PREV
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				add_to_faction = TEX
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TEX_austrian_prince
				AUS = {
					exists = yes
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				TEX = {
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				add_to_faction = TEX
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TEX_austrian_prince
				AUS = {
					exists = yes
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
				TEX = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			TEX = {
				add_to_faction = AUS
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TEX_spanish_prince
				SPR = {
					exists = yes
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				TEX = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = TEX
					NOT = {
						is_subject_of = TEX
					}
				}
				SPR = {
				add_to_faction = PREV
				}
			}
			SPR = {
				add_to_faction = TEX
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TEX_spanish_prince
				SPR = {
					exists = yes
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				TEX = {
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
			}
			SPR = {
				add_to_faction = TEX
			}
		}

				}

country_event = { # should we?
	id = unionstatefp.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event cathdeath.102" }
	title = unionstatefp.1.t
	desc = unionstatefp.1.d
	picture = GFX_ACW_civil_war

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #sure
		name = unionstatefp.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TEX_foreign_policy
					option = TEX_FOREIGN_POLICY_AMERICANISM
				}
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = {
				id = unionstatefp.2
				days = 2
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = { #no
		name = unionstatefp.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TEX_foreign_policy
					option = TEX_FOREIGN_POLICY_REICHSPAKT
				}
			}
		}
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		
	}
}

country_event = { # TEX wants to join us
	id = unionstatefp.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event cathdeath.102" }
	title = unionstatefp.2.t
	desc = unionstatefp.2.d
	picture = GFX_ACW_civil_war

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #sure
		name = unionstatefp.2.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = unionstatefp.3
				days = 2
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = { #no
		name = unionstatefp.2.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				FROM = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				is_ai = no
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TEX_foreign_policy
					option = TEX_FOREIGN_POLICY_REICHSPAKT
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = unionstatefp.4
				days = 2
			}
		}
		
	}
}

		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FOP
			modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FOP
			modifier = KR_trade_agreement
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FOP
			modifier = KR_trade_agreement
		}
	}
	option = { #Invite them into the faction
		name = unionstatefp.5.c
		trigger = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
		}
		FOP = {
			country_event = {
				id = unionstatefp.6
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}
